# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENT 006 INDEPENDENCE WAVE EFFECTS
# ============================================================================
# Foundation effects for the instant Independence Wave resolver. These helpers
# deliberately use Event 006 origin flags and do not read Event 005 state.
# ============================================================================

@independence_wave_host_recent_days = 240
@independence_wave_breakaway_recent_days = 240
@independence_wave_patron_ledger_cooldown_days = 75
@independence_wave_compact_refusal_cooldown_days = 90
@independence_wave_border_cooldown_days = 90
@independence_wave_oil_resource_gate = 0
@independence_wave_startup_guard_divisions = 2
@independence_wave_local_defense_brigade_divisions = 1

independence_wave_build_capital_railway_to_this_state = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { is_capital = yes }
			ROOT = {
				any_owned_state = {
					is_capital = yes
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { ROOT.independence_wave_temp_rail_target_state = THIS.id }
		ROOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				set_variable = { ROOT.independence_wave_temp_rail_start_state = THIS.id }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					can_build_railway = {
						level = 1
						build_only_on_allied = yes
						fallback = yes
						start_state = var:ROOT.independence_wave_temp_rail_start_state
						target_state = var:ROOT.independence_wave_temp_rail_target_state
					}
				}
				build_railway = {
					level = 1
					build_only_on_allied = yes
					fallback = yes
					start_state = var:ROOT.independence_wave_temp_rail_start_state
					target_state = var:ROOT.independence_wave_temp_rail_target_state
				}
			}
			clear_variable = independence_wave_temp_rail_start_state
			clear_variable = independence_wave_temp_rail_target_state
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_ensure_emergency_equipment_variants = {
	set_technology = {
		infantry_weapons = 1
		infantry_weapons1 = 1
		tech_support = 1
		tech_engineers = 1
		artillery1 = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_emergency_equipment_variants_registered } }
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_emergency_equipment_variants_registered
		create_equipment_variant = {
			name = "Dossier Committee Rifles"
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			allow_without_tech = yes
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			name = "Dossier Committee Stores"
			type = support_equipment_1
			allow_without_tech = yes
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			name = "Dossier Committee Field Guns"
			type = artillery_equipment_1
			allow_without_tech = yes
		}
		create_equipment_variant = {
			name = "Dossier Committee Rail Stock"
			type = train_equipment_1
			allow_without_tech = yes
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_prepare_release_count = {
	add_to_variable = { global.independence_wave_wave_serial = 1 }
	set_variable = { global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_min = constant:independence_wave_release_count.baseline_min }
	set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_max_exclusive = constant:independence_wave_release_count.baseline_max_exclusive }
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 1 } }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_min = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_1_min }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_max_exclusive = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_1_max_exclusive }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.gathering_storm_stage }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 } }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_min = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_2_min }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_max_exclusive = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_2_max_exclusive }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.rising_cascade_stage }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 } }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_min = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_3_min }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_max_exclusive = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_3_max_exclusive }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.old_names_stage }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_min = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_4_min }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_max_exclusive = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_4_max_exclusive }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.impossible_statehood_stage }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_min = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_5_min }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_count_max_exclusive = constant:independence_wave_release_count.evo_5_max_exclusive }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.world_collapse_stage }
	}
	set_variable_to_random = {
		var = global.independence_wave_release_count_target
		min = independence_wave_release_count_min
		max = independence_wave_release_count_max_exclusive
		integer = yes
	}
	set_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 0 }
	set_variable = { global.chaosx_iw_current_wave_host_count = 0 }
	clr_global_flag = independence_wave_current_wave_special_package
	clr_global_flag = independence_wave_current_wave_major_host_partitioned
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_1
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_2
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_3
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_4
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_5
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_6
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_7
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_8
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_9
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_10
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_11
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_12
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_13
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_14
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_15
	clear_variable = global.independence_wave_country_16
	clear_array = global.independence_wave_candidate_pool
	clear_array = global.independence_wave_current_wave_releases
}

independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			can_independence_wave_candidate_enter_ordinary_pool = yes
			NOT = { is_in_array = { array = global.independence_wave_candidate_pool value = THIS } }
		}
		add_to_array = { array = global.independence_wave_candidate_pool value = THIS }
	}
}

independence_wave_seed_niche_generic_candidates = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		KAT = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		BIA = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		CBV = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		RIF = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		RAP = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		RIG = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		WLA = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		HAR = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		TIG = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		AFA = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		BEG = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		GBA = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		SID = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		ORO = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		QEM = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		274 = {
			add_core_of = ASN
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_asante_generic_core_seeded
		}
		ASN = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		774 = {
			add_core_of = KBN
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_kanem_bornu_generic_core_seeded
		}
		901 = {
			add_core_of = KBN
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_kanem_bornu_generic_core_seeded
		}
		KBN = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		936 = {
			add_core_of = PLM
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_palmares_generic_core_seeded
		}
		498 = {
			add_core_of = PLM
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_palmares_generic_core_seeded
		}
		PLM = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
		947 = {
			add_core_of = AYM
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_aymara_generic_core_seeded
		}
		951 = {
			add_core_of = AYM
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_aymara_generic_core_seeded
		}
		506 = {
			add_core_of = AYM
			set_state_flag = independence_wave_aymara_generic_core_seeded
		}
		AYM = { independence_wave_add_current_candidate_if_eligible = yes }
	}
}

	independence_wave_reserve_host_survival_state = {
		if = { limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_protected_host_state } clear_global_event_target = independence_wave_protected_host_state }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_candidate
			capital_scope = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		capital_scope = {
			save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_protected_host_state
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_candidate
			NOT = { has_event_target = independence_wave_protected_host_state }
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate }
				OR = {
					industrial_complex > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
					arms_factory > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
					dockyard > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
					supply_node > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_protected_host_state
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_candidate
			NOT = { has_event_target = independence_wave_protected_host_state }
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate }
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					has_state_category = city
					has_state_category = large_city
					has_state_category = metropolis
					has_state_category = megalopolis
					infrastructure > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_infrastructure_gate
				}
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_protected_host_state
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_candidate
			NOT = { has_event_target = independence_wave_protected_host_state }
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate }
			}
			save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_protected_host_state
		}
	}
}

	independence_wave_prepare_reduced_release_footprint = {
		if = { limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state } clear_global_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
	independence_wave_try_package_reduced_release_anchor = yes
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host }
		event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					is_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate
					NOT = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_host_survival_reserved }
					OR = {
						industrial_complex > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
						arms_factory > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
						dockyard > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
						supply_node > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_building_floor
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor
				save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host
			NOT = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
		}
		event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					is_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate
					NOT = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_host_survival_reserved }
					OR = {
						is_core_of = PREV
						has_state_category = city
						has_state_category = large_city
						has_state_category = metropolis
						has_state_category = megalopolis
						infrastructure > constant:independence_wave_resolver.protected_state_infrastructure_gate
					}
				}
				set_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor
				save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host
			NOT = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
		}
		event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = PREV
					is_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate
					NOT = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_host_survival_reserved }
				}
				set_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor
				save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
		event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate
					NOT = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor }
				}
				remove_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate
				set_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_core_masked
			}
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_restore_reduced_release_cores = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host
			event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_core_masked
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_reduced_territory_start
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_border_survey_filed
		add_to_variable = { independence_wave_claim_ambition = constant:independence_wave_startup.reduced_start_claim_ambition_gain }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host }
		event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_core_masked }
				add_core_of = event_target:independence_wave_current_candidate
				clr_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_core_masked
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
		event_target:independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state = {
			clr_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor
		}
	}
		if = { limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state } clear_global_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
}

independence_wave_try_package_reduced_release_anchor = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = OGB
			has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host
			NOT = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
		}
		event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
			249 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = PREV
						is_owned_by = PREV
						is_core_of = ROOT
						NOT = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_host_survival_reserved }
					}
					set_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor
					save_global_event_target_as = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			tag = OGB

				463 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				864 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				472 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				683 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				466 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				332 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				101 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				861 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } remove_core_of = INU clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { INU = { exists = yes } }
				463 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }
				864 = { if = { limit = { has_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } clr_state_flag = independence_wave_inuit_package_core_seeded } }

independence_wave_clear_pending_candidate_state = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
		event_target:independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state = {
			clr_state_flag = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor
		}
	}
		if = { limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_protected_host_state } clear_global_event_target = independence_wave_protected_host_state }
		if = { limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host } clear_global_event_target = independence_wave_current_host }
		if = { limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state } clear_global_event_target = independence_wave_reduced_release_anchor_state }
}

independence_wave_prepare_host_wave_tracking = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_host_pre_wave_tracking_id value = global.independence_wave_wave_serial compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { independence_wave_host_pre_wave_tracking_id = global.independence_wave_wave_serial }
		set_variable = { independence_wave_host_pre_wave_controlled_states = num_of_controlled_states }
	}
}

independence_wave_mark_host_aftermath = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_host_counted_wave_id value = global.independence_wave_wave_serial compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
		set_variable = { independence_wave_host_counted_wave_id = global.independence_wave_wave_serial }
		set_variable = { independence_wave_host_current_wave_release_loss_count = 0 }
		add_to_variable = { global.chaosx_iw_current_wave_host_count = 1 }
	}
	add_to_variable = { independence_wave_host_current_wave_release_loss_count = 1 }
	set_country_flag = {
		flag = independence_wave_recent_host
		days = @independence_wave_host_recent_days
	}
	set_country_flag = independence_wave_host_aftermath_open
	set_variable = { independence_wave_host_survival_floor = constant:independence_wave_resolver.host_survival_state_floor }
	add_to_variable = { independence_wave_host_anger = constant:independence_wave_startup.host_anger_gain }
	if = {
		limit = {
			capital_scope = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_host_kept_capital
	}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_host_kept_capital
				check_variable = {
					var = independence_wave_host_current_wave_release_loss_count
					value = constant:independence_wave_achievement.capital_survival_release_losses_required
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_capital_still_answers
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_host_suppressed_first
				check_variable = {
					var = global.independence_wave_wave_serial
					value = chaosx_iw_suppression_wave_serial
					compare = greater_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = independence_wave_host_current_wave_release_loss_count
					value = constant:independence_wave_achievement.suppression_later_release_losses_required
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_later_breakaways_lost_by_host
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_major = yes
				check_variable = {
					var = independence_wave_host_current_wave_release_loss_count
					value = constant:independence_wave_achievement.great_partition_major_host_losses_required
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_current_wave_major_host_partitioned
		}
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_active_mission = independence_wave_hold_capital_ministry } }
			activate_mission = independence_wave_hold_capital_ministry
		}
		independence_wave_show_host_rump_report_once = yes
		independence_wave_show_rump_that_endures_super_event = yes
	}

		set_country_flag = independence_wave_parent_negotiation_attempted
		add_to_variable = { independence_wave_claim_ambition = constant:independence_wave_decision.host_border_negotiation_claim_relief }
		add_to_variable = { independence_wave_legitimacy = constant:independence_wave_decision.host_border_negotiation_legitimacy_gain }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_claim_ambition value = constant:independence_wave_decision.border_claim_ambition_floor compare = less_than }
			}
			set_variable = { independence_wave_claim_ambition = constant:independence_wave_decision.border_claim_ambition_floor }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_claim_ambition value = constant:independence_wave_decision.host_border_reclamation_claim_gate compare = greater_than }
			}
			set_country_flag = independence_wave_parent_negotiation_failed
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					check_variable = { var = independence_wave_claim_ambition value = constant:independence_wave_decision.host_border_reclamation_claim_gate compare = greater_than }
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = independence_wave_parent_response_pending
			set_country_flag = independence_wave_parent_negotiation_success
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_mark_limited_territory_start = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			num_of_controlled_states > 0
			num_of_controlled_states < constant:independence_wave_decision.compact_required_states
		}
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_limited_territory_start
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_border_survey_filed
		add_to_variable = { independence_wave_claim_ambition = constant:independence_wave_startup.reduced_start_claim_ambition_gain }
	}
}

		set_country_flag = independence_wave_ordinary_release

		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_protectorate_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_historical_return_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_local_polity_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_strange_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_free_port_authority

		clear_variable = chaosx_independence_wave_formable_family

		set_variable = { independence_wave_package_id = constant:independence_wave_package.ordinary }
		remove_ideas = independence_wave_free_city_board_spirit
		remove_ideas = independence_wave_canal_authority_spirit
		remove_ideas = independence_wave_municipal_authority_spirit
		remove_ideas = independence_wave_oil_protectorate_spirit

	if = {
		limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 1 } }

		set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_dormant_candidate

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 }

			set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_city_or_port

		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_ordinary_release
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_charrua
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_local_polity_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_historical_return_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_strange_candidate
		independence_wave_clear_strange_package_identity = yes
		set_variable = { independence_wave_package_id = constant:independence_wave_package.charrua }
		set_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.local_polity_package }
		set_variable = { chaosx_independence_wave_formable_family = constant:independence_wave_decision.formation_family_land_congress }
		add_to_variable = { independence_wave_local_polity_cohesion = constant:independence_wave_focus.local_polity_gain }
		add_ideas = independence_wave_charrua_memory_assembly_spirit
	}
	if = {
		limit = { tag = KUR }
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_ordinary_release
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_kurdistan
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_local_polity_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_historical_return_candidate
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_strange_candidate
		independence_wave_clear_strange_package_identity = yes
		set_variable = { independence_wave_package_id = constant:independence_wave_package.kurdistan }
		set_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.local_polity_package }
		set_variable = { chaosx_independence_wave_formable_family = constant:independence_wave_decision.formation_family_mountain_assembly }
		add_to_variable = { independence_wave_local_polity_cohesion = constant:independence_wave_focus.local_polity_gain }
		add_ideas = independence_wave_kurdish_mountain_assembly_spirit
	}
}

independence_wave_classify_strange_package_identity = {
	set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_archive_state
	clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_necromantic_custodianship
	set_variable = { independence_wave_package_id = constant:independence_wave_package.archive_state }
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					has_state_category = rural
					has_state_category = pastoral
					has_state_category = wasteland
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_city_or_port }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_railway_candidate }
		}
		clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_archive_state
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_package_necromantic_custodianship
		set_variable = { independence_wave_package_id = constant:independence_wave_package.necromantic_custodianship }
	}
}

independence_wave_clear_strange_package_identity = {
	clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_archive_state
	clr_country_flag = independence_wave_package_necromantic_custodianship
}

independence_wave_update_achievement_tracking = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_independence_wave_release = yes }
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_achievement_valid_origin
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_patron_accepted } }
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_no_patron_accepted
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_puppet_status_ever
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_historical_return_candidate
					has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_volga_bulgaria
					has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_assyria
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_sokoto
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_bukhara
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_khiva
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_dahomey
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_historical_return_package
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_historical_return_package
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chaosx_iw_first_old_name_seen }
			}
			set_global_flag = chaosx_iw_first_old_name_seen
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_first_old_name_country
			independence_wave_show_first_old_name_super_event = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_local_polity_candidate
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_buganda
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_barotseland
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_guarani
						has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_charrua
					has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_kurdistan
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_local_polity_package
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_strange_candidate }
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_strange_package
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_strange_package
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chaosx_iw_first_impossible_state_seen }
				NOT = { has_global_flag = chaosx_iw_world_end_bypass_used }
				is_subject = no
			}
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_first_impossible_state_country
			independence_wave_show_first_impossible_state_super_event = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_railway_candidate }
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_railway_package
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_emit_super_event = {
	set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_super_event_visible_days = constant:independence_wave_super_event.visible_days }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = super_event_visible
				days = independence_wave_super_event_visible_days
				value = [SUPER_EVENT_ID]
			}
		}
		SUPER_EVENT_ID = "[?independence_wave_super_event_id|.0]"
	}
	set_variable = { global.current_super_event_audio_id = independence_wave_super_event_id }
	every_country = {
		limit = { is_ai = no }
		play_current_super_event_audio = yes
	}
}

independence_wave_show_first_league_super_event = {
	if = {
		limit = { can_independence_wave_show_first_league_super_event = yes }
		set_global_flag = independence_wave_first_league_super_event_fired
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_super_event_id = constant:independence_wave_super_event.first_league }
		independence_wave_emit_super_event = yes
	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_super_event_id = constant:independence_wave_super_event.human_renunciation }

	}
}

		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_super_event_id = constant:independence_wave_super_event.first_impossible_state }
		independence_wave_emit_super_event = yes
	}
}

independence_wave_show_league_war_super_event = {
	if = {
		limit = { can_independence_wave_show_league_war_super_event = yes }
		set_global_flag = independence_wave_league_war_super_event_fired

		independence_wave_emit_super_event = yes
	}
}

independence_wave_mark_league_war_members = {
	set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_at_start
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.independence_wave_compact_members
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = yes
				is_independence_wave_release = yes
				has_country_flag = independence_wave_compact_member
			}
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_at_start
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_mark_league_war_against_from = {
	if = {
		limit = { can_independence_wave_start_league_war_against_from = yes }
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active_founder
		set_global_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active
		save_global_event_target_as = chaosx_iw_league_war_founder
		independence_wave_mark_league_war_members = yes
		FROM = {
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy_target
			save_global_event_target_as = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy
		}
		independence_wave_show_league_war_super_event = yes
	}
}

independence_wave_mark_league_war_against_root = {
	if = {
		limit = { can_independence_wave_start_league_war_against_root = yes }
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active_founder
		set_global_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active
		save_global_event_target_as = chaosx_iw_league_war_founder
		independence_wave_mark_league_war_members = yes
		ROOT = {
			set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy_target
			save_global_event_target_as = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy
		}
		independence_wave_show_league_war_super_event = yes
	}
}

independence_wave_fail_active_league_war = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active_founder }
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_failed
		clr_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active_founder
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy }
		event_target:chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy = {
			clr_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy_target
		}
	}
	clr_global_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active
	clear_global_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_founder
	clear_global_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy
}

independence_wave_fail_active_league_war_from_loss = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active_founder
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_at_start
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_failed
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_founder }
		event_target:chaosx_iw_league_war_founder = {
			independence_wave_fail_active_league_war = yes
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_fail_active_league_war_from_puppet = {
	set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_puppet_status_ever
	independence_wave_fail_active_league_war_from_loss = yes
}

independence_wave_mark_league_war_victory_if_clean = {
	clr_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_loss_detected
	set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_league_war_victory_valid = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active_founder }
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_failed
				is_subject = yes
				has_capitulated = yes
				has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_puppet_status_ever
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_league_war_victory_valid = 0 }
	}
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.independence_wave_compact_members
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = yes }
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_at_start
						OR = {
							is_subject = yes
							has_capitulated = yes
							has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_puppet_status_ever
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = { set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_loss_detected }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_loss_detected }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_league_war_victory_valid = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = independence_wave_league_war_victory_valid value = 1 compare = equals } }
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_victory_confirmed
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_founders_remained_free
		set_global_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_victory_confirmed
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = independence_wave_league_war_victory_valid value = 1 compare = not_equals } }
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_failed
	}
	clr_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active_founder
	clr_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_member_loss_detected
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy }
		event_target:chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy = {
			clr_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy_target
		}
	}
	clr_global_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_active
	clear_global_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_founder
	clear_global_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy
}

independence_wave_resolve_league_war_enemy_defeat = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_league_war_enemy_target
			has_event_target = chaosx_iw_league_war_founder
		}
		event_target:chaosx_iw_league_war_founder = {
			independence_wave_mark_league_war_victory_if_clean = yes
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_add_compact_members_to_faction = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_in_faction = yes
			is_faction_leader = yes
		}
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.independence_wave_compact_members
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					is_independence_wave_release = yes
					has_country_flag = independence_wave_compact_member
					is_subject = no
					is_in_faction = no
					NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

	independence_wave_form_regional_compact = {
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_regional_compact_formed
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_founded_league
		set_global_flag = chaosx_iw_founded_league
		independence_wave_show_league_report_once = yes
	set_country_flag = chaosx_formation_origin_independence_wave
	set_variable = { chaosx_independence_wave_formable_family = constant:independence_wave_decision.formation_family_regional }
	set_variable = { global.chaosx_iw_league_member_count = independence_wave_compact_member_count }
	remove_ideas = independence_wave_regional_compact_preparation_spirit
	add_ideas = independence_wave_regional_compact_spirit
	add_to_variable = { independence_wave_coalition_cohesion = constant:independence_wave_decision.compact_cohesion_gain }
	add_to_variable = { independence_wave_legitimacy = constant:independence_wave_decision.compact_legitimacy_gain }
	add_to_variable = { independence_wave_pressure = constant:independence_wave_decision.compact_pressure_relief }
	if = {
		limit = { is_in_faction = no }
		set_rule = { can_create_factions = yes }
		create_faction = independence_wave_new_states_compact_faction
	}
	independence_wave_add_compact_members_to_faction = yes
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_active_mission = independence_wave_integrate_compact_ministries } }
		activate_mission = independence_wave_integrate_compact_ministries
	}
	independence_wave_mark_charter_not_chains_if_clean = yes
	independence_wave_show_first_league_super_event = yes
}

independence_wave_mark_charter_not_chains_if_clean = {
	set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_charter_not_chains_valid = 1 }
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_compact_anti_puppet_clause } }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_charter_not_chains_valid = 0 }
	}
	for_each_scope_loop = {
		array = global.independence_wave_compact_members
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = { exists = yes }
					NOT = { is_independence_wave_release = yes }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_compact_member }
					is_subject = yes
					has_country_flag = chaosx_iw_puppet_status_ever
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_charter_not_chains_valid = 0 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { var = independence_wave_charter_not_chains_valid value = 1 compare = equals } }
		set_country_flag = chaosx_iw_charter_not_chains
	}
}

independence_wave_prepare_event_log_tier = {
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 0 }
	if = { limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 1 } } set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 1 } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 } } set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 2 } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 } } set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 3 } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } } set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 4 } }
	if = { limit = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } } set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 5 } }
}

independence_wave_record_release_scale_evolution_entry = {
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_event_id = constant:independence_wave_event_log.event_id }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.evolution_type }
	if = {
		limit = { is_current_evolution_enabled = yes }
		record_events_log_evolution_entry = yes
	}
}

independence_wave_set_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown = {
	set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown_days = constant:independence_wave_evolution_mtth.check_cooldown_days }
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			set_global_flag = {
				flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown
				days = [EVOLUTION_CHECK_COOLDOWN_DAYS]
			}
		}
		EVOLUTION_CHECK_COOLDOWN_DAYS = "[?independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown_days|.0]"
	}
}

independence_wave_roll_release_scale_evolution_entry = {
	clr_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded
	if = {
		limit = { is_current_evolution_enabled = yes }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_weight = mtth:independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_weight }
		set_temp_variable = { independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_miss_weight = constant:independence_wave_evolution_mtth.miss_base }
		independence_wave_set_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown = yes
		random_list = {
			seed = random
			independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_weight = {
				independence_wave_record_release_scale_evolution_entry = yes
				set_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded
			}
			independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_miss_weight = { }
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_record_tier_evolution_log_entry = {
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_event_id = constant:independence_wave_event_log.event_id }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.evolution_type }
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_gathering_storm_milestone_logged }
			has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 1 }
			check_variable = { var = global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage value = constant:independence_wave_event_log.gathering_storm_stage compare = equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.gathering_storm_stage }
		independence_wave_roll_release_scale_evolution_entry = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded }
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_gathering_storm_milestone_logged
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_gathering_storm_logged
			clr_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_rising_cascade_milestone_logged }
			has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 2 }
			check_variable = { var = global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage value = constant:independence_wave_event_log.rising_cascade_stage compare = equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.rising_cascade_stage }
		independence_wave_roll_release_scale_evolution_entry = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded }
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_rising_cascade_milestone_logged
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_rising_cascade_logged
			clr_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_old_names_milestone_logged }
			has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
			check_variable = { var = global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage value = constant:independence_wave_event_log.old_names_stage compare = equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 3 }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.old_names_stage }
		independence_wave_roll_release_scale_evolution_entry = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded }
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_old_names_milestone_logged
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_old_names_logged
			clr_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_impossible_statehood_milestone_logged }
			has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
			check_variable = { var = global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage value = constant:independence_wave_event_log.impossible_statehood_stage compare = equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 4 }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.impossible_statehood_stage }
		independence_wave_roll_release_scale_evolution_entry = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded }
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_impossible_statehood_milestone_logged
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_impossible_statehood_logged
			clr_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_check_cooldown }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_world_collapse_milestone_logged }
			has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			check_variable = { var = global.independence_wave_release_scale_stage value = constant:independence_wave_event_log.world_collapse_stage compare = equals }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_tier = 5 }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.world_collapse_stage }
		independence_wave_roll_release_scale_evolution_entry = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded }
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_world_collapse_milestone_logged
			set_global_flag = independence_wave_evolution_world_collapse_logged
			clr_country_flag = independence_wave_release_scale_evolution_roll_succeeded
		}
	}
}

independence_wave_record_release_dossier_log_entry = {
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_event_id = constant:independence_wave_event_log.event_id }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.ordinary_dossier_type }
	set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_stage = constant:independence_wave_event_log.dossier_stage }
	independence_wave_prepare_event_log_tier = yes
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.dormant_package } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.dormant_dossier_type }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.city_package } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.city_dossier_type }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.protectorate_package } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.protectorate_dossier_type }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.railway_package } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.railway_dossier_type }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.historical_return_package } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.historical_return_dossier_type }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.local_polity_package } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.local_polity_dossier_type }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { independence_wave_package_type = constant:independence_wave_startup.strange_package } }
		set_temp_variable = { events_log_evolution_type = constant:independence_wave_event_log.strange_dossier_type }
	}

independence_wave_register_successful_release = {
	add_to_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 1 }
	add_to_array = { array = global.independence_wave_released_countries value = THIS }
	add_to_array = { array = global.independence_wave_current_wave_releases value = THIS }
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_city_candidate
				has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_railway_candidate
				has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_historical_return_candidate
				has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_local_polity_candidate
				has_country_flag = independence_wave_package_strange_candidate
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_package_type value = constant:independence_wave_startup.city_package compare = equals }
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_package_type value = constant:independence_wave_startup.railway_package compare = equals }
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_package_type value = constant:independence_wave_startup.historical_return_package compare = equals }
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_package_type value = constant:independence_wave_startup.local_polity_package compare = equals }
				check_variable = { var = independence_wave_package_type value = constant:independence_wave_startup.strange_package compare = equals }
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = independence_wave_current_wave_special_package
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_event_target = independence_wave_current_host }
		event_target:independence_wave_current_host = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_in_array = { array = independence_wave_host_released_countries value = PREV } }
				}
				add_to_array = { array = independence_wave_host_released_countries value = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 1 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_1 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 2 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_2 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 3 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_3 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 4 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_4 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 5 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_5 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 6 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_6 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 7 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_7 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 8 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_8 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 9 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_9 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 10 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_10 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 11 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_11 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 12 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_12 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 13 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_13 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 14 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_14 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 15 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_15 = THIS.id }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { global.independence_wave_actual_release_count = 16 } }
		set_variable = { global.independence_wave_country_16 = THIS.id }
	}
}

independence_wave_open_congress_if_ready = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_independence_wave_release = yes
			check_variable = { var = global.independence_wave_actual_release_count value = 1 compare = greater_than }
		}
		set_country_flag = independence_wave_new_states_congress_open
	}
}
